# Qubit Characterization Workflow

Reference implementation: `/Users/baqis/autolab/characterize.py`
Run any step with: `uv run python characterize.py <step>`

---

## Step Sequence

```
init_qsync вҶ’ trace вҶ’ s21 вҶ’ readout_snr вҶ’ spectrum вҶ’ power_rabi вҶ’ time_rabi
  вҶ’ single_shot вҶ’ ramsey вҶ’ t1 вҶ’ r12 вҶ’ summary
```

For a full run: `uv run python characterize.py all`

Alternatively, run `s21_readout_snr` to chain S21 cavity detection into SNR
optimization in a single step.

---

## Step-by-Step Reference

### 0a. `init_qsync` вҖ” Initialize trigger
Sets NS_QSYNC trigger period to 200 Вөs, RefClock to internal, issues SystemSync.
Run once at the start of each session.

### 0b. `trace` вҖ” ADC trace / TRIGD alignment
Captures raw ADC trace to verify the measurement window is correctly aligned.
Plot the trace and check that the readout pulse falls inside the integration window.
Adjust `acquire.TRIGD` or `Measure.weight` offset if misaligned.

### 1. `s21` вҖ” Readout cavity
Sweeps `Measure.frequency` Вұ5 MHz around the current center at fixed amp.

**CRITICAL вҖ” find the DIP, not the peak.**
The cavity appears as a transmission minimum in S21:
```python
# Correct
peaks, props = find_peaks(-s21, prominence=np.std(s21) * 0.3)
cavity_freq = xaxis[peaks[np.argmax(props['prominences'])]]
# Fallback if no peak found
cavity_freq = xaxis[np.argmin(s21)]
```
Using `find_peaks(s21, ...)` finds the background maximum вҖ” wrong.

### 2. `readout_snr` вҖ” 2D readout parameter optimization
**This is the primary readout calibration step.** Scans `Measure.frequency Г—
Measure.amp` and maximizes IQ SNR.

**SNR definition:**
```
signal = |mean(IQ|1вҹ©) вҲ’ mean(IQ|0вҹ©)|   # distance between IQ cloud centers
noise  = (std(IQ|0вҹ©) + std(IQ|1вҹ©)) / 2  # average single-shot spread
SNR    = signal / (noise + 1e-12)
```

**Signal type:** always `signal='iq'` (not `iq_avg`, not `population`).

**Data shape** with `signal='iq'`:
```
(n_state, n_freq, n_amp, n_shots, n_qubits)
```
Extract qubit 0: `iq = data[..., 0]` вҶ’ shape `(n_state, n_freq, n_amp, n_shots)`

**Known anomaly вҖ” measurement-induced transitions:**
Near the cavity frequency at high readout power, the qubit can be excited by
readout photons. This appears as a region in the 2D SNR map where:
- noise is anomalously high (ПғвӮҖ, ПғвӮҒ both large)
- signal is near zero (IQ clouds overlap or swap)
The true optimum is just outside this region.

**Boundary-hitting:** If best amp = 1.0 (scan maximum), the SNR has not saturated
within the scanned range. This is expected вҖ” measurement-induced transitions set a
physical upper limit. It is not a bug.

**Combined step:** `s21_readout_snr` runs S21 first (finds cavity DIP), then
immediately runs the 2D SNR scan centered on the cavity frequency.

### 3. `spectrum` вҖ” Qubit spectroscopy (f01)
Sweeps `R.frequency` at high drive amp and long width to find the |0вҹ©вҶ’|1вҹ© transition.
Updates `R.frequency` to the peak position.
Use `signal='iq_avg'`.

### 4. `power_rabi` вҖ” ПҖ pulse amplitude
Sweeps `R.amp` at fixed width (100 ns). Fit gives ПҖ_amp = 0.5 / f_Rabi.
Updates `R.amp`.
Use `signal='iq_avg'`.

### 5. `time_rabi` вҖ” ПҖ pulse width
Sweeps `R.width` at fixed amp (1.0 by default) or at the calibrated ПҖ amp.
Fit gives ПҖ_width.
Updates `R.width`.
Use `signal='iq_avg'`.

### 6. `single_shot` вҖ” Readout threshold calibration
**Must run before using `signal='population'` anywhere.**
Prepares |0вҹ© and |1вҹ©, collects IQ shots, computes:
- `Measure.threshold` вҖ” decision boundary in rotated IQ frame
- `Measure.phi` вҖ” IQ rotation angle
- `Measure.PgPe` вҖ” readout error matrix

Updates config immediately. If readout parameters (frequency, amp) change after
this step, re-run `single_shot` to recalibrate.

### 7. `ramsey` вҖ” T2* and frequency refinement
Ramsey fringe with variable free-evolution delay. Fit gives T2* and frequency
detuning О”f. Corrects `R.frequency` and records `params.T2_star`.

### 8. `t1` вҖ” Energy relaxation
Exponential decay after ПҖ pulse. Fit gives T1. Records `params.T1`.
Use log-spaced delays for wide dynamic range.

### 9. `r12` вҖ” |1вҹ©вҶ’|2вҹ© transition
Two sub-steps:
- **Spectrum12**: sweeps `R12.frequency` to find f12. Updates `R12.frequency`.
- **PowerRabi12**: sweeps `R12.amp` to calibrate ПҖ12 pulse. Updates `R12.amp`.
Uses `signal='population'` вҖ” requires prior `single_shot` calibration.

---

## Signal Type Rules

| Use case | Correct signal | Why |
|---|---|---|
| SNR optimization | `'iq'` | Need shot-by-shot variance |
| SingleShot calibration | `'iq'` | Need raw clouds for threshold fit |
| Spectroscopy / Rabi | `'iq_avg'` | Averaged phase/amp is sufficient |
| Population-based fits | `'population'` | Only after single_shot calibration |

**`signal='population'` flat-line diagnosis:**
If time_rabi or other population-signal experiments give a flat line near 0.5:
1. Check that `single_shot` was run after the current readout parameters were set.
2. Verify `Measure.threshold` and `Measure.phi` are non-trivial in config.
3. Re-run `single_shot`, then repeat the failing step.

---

## Data Shape Convention

For `signal='iq'`, axes follow recipe sweep order with shots second-to-last and
qubits last:
```
(sweep_axis_0, sweep_axis_1, ..., n_shots, n_qubits)
```

Examples:
- SingleShot with `[state, repeat]`: `(n_state, n_repeat, n_shots, n_qubits)`
- ReadoutSNR with `[state, freq, amp]`: `(n_state, n_freq, n_amp, n_shots, n_qubits)`

Always index `[..., 0]` to extract qubit 0 before computing statistics.

---

## Matplotlib / Plotting

Use English-only labels in all plot calls. CJK characters cause:
```
UserWarning: Glyph XXXX missing from font(s) DejaVu Sans
```
Replace Chinese strings with English equivalents:
- `'е№…еәҰ'` вҶ’ `'Amplitude'`
- `'йў‘зҺҮ'` вҶ’ `'Frequency (GHz)'`
- `'дҝЎеҷӘжҜ”'` вҶ’ `'SNR'`
- `'иҜ»еҮәи…”йў‘зҺҮ'` вҶ’ `'Readout cavity frequency'`

---

## Common Troubleshooting

| Symptom | Likely cause | Fix |
|---|---|---|
| S21 shows no dip, only a broad peak | Using `find_peaks(s21)` instead of `find_peaks(-s21)` | Fix peak detection |
| ReadoutSNR best amp = 1.0 | SNR not saturated within scan range; physical limit from measurement-induced transitions | Acceptable; consider using amp slightly below boundary |
| Max-noise region in SNR map near cavity freq at low amp | Measurement-induced transitions | Avoid that region; choose params outside it |
| Population signal flat at ~0.5 | `single_shot` not run after readout parameter change | Re-run `single_shot` |
| Rabi fit fails | Low contrast, wrong frequency, or signal type mismatch | Check `R.frequency` with spectrum first; verify signal type |
| Task fails immediately | Hardware not initialized | Run `init_qsync` first |

---

## Config Keys Reference (Q0)

| Config path | Parameter | Typical value |
|---|---|---|
| `Q0.R.frequency` | Drive freq f01 | ~3.82 GHz |
| `Q0.R.amp` | ПҖ pulse amp | 0.83 |
| `Q0.R.width` | ПҖ pulse width | 100 ns |
| `Q0.Measure.frequency` | Readout freq | ~7.000 GHz |
| `Q0.Measure.amp` | Readout amp | ~0.99 |
| `Q0.Measure.threshold` | IQ decision boundary | device-specific |
| `Q0.Measure.phi` | IQ rotation angle (rad) | device-specific |
| `Q0.Measure.PgPe` | Readout error [1вҲ’Fg, 1вҲ’Fe] | device-specific |
| `Q0.acquire.TRIGD` | ADC trigger delay | ~220 ns |
| `Q0.params.T1` | T1 (s) | ~20 Вөs |

Read: `s.query('Q0.Measure.frequency')`
Write: `s.update('Q0.Measure.frequency', value)`

284	
285	    print('  TrigFrom  = 0 (еҶ…йғЁ)')
286	    print('  RefClock  = in')
287	    print('  TrigPeriod= 800 Ојs')
288	    print('  вң“ NS_QSYNC еҲқе§ӢеҢ–е®ҢжҲҗ')
289	
290	
291	# в”Җв”Җв”Җ 0c. ADC Trace / TRIGD еҜ№йҪҗ в”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җ
292	
293	def step_trace():
294	    print('\n' + '='*55)
295	    print('жӯҘйӘӨ 0b / ADC Trace вҖ” еҜ№йҪҗ TRIGD')
296	    print('='*55)
297	
298	    trigd = s.query(f'{QUBIT}.acquire.TRIGD')
299	    print(f'  еҪ“еүҚ TRIGD = {trigd} s')
300	    print(f'  Measure.duration = {s.query(f"{QUBIT}.Measure.duration")*1e6:.2f} Ојs')
301	    print(f'  Measure.weight   = {s.query(f"{QUBIT}.Measure.weight")}')
302	
303	    rcp = Recipe('trace', signal='trace')
304	    rcp.circuit = circuit_trace
305	    rcp['qubits'] = QUBITS
306	    rcp['repeat'] = list(range(200))
307	    rcp[f'{QUBIT}.Measure.frequency'] = 7.1e9
308	    rcp[f'{QUBIT}.Measure.amp'] = 1
309	
310	    task = s.submit(rcp.export(), block=True, preview=[], plot=False)
311	    task.bar(interval=0.1)
312	    print(f'  RID = {task.rid}')
313	
314	    if task.status()['status'] == 'Failed':
315	        print('  вң— д»»еҠЎеӨұиҙҘпјҢиҜ·жЈҖжҹҘ server ж—Ҙеҝ—')
316	        return None
317	
318	    result    = get_data_by_rid(task.rid)
319	    signal    = result['meta']['other']['signal']
320	    traces    = np.array(result['data'][signal])
321	    print(f'  trace shape = {traces.shape} {traces.dtype}')
322	    y = np.mean(traces[:,:,0,0], axis=0)
323	    x = np.arange(len(y)) / 4
324	    plt.plot(x, y)
325	    plt.xlabel('Time [ns]')
326	    savefig('00_trace')
327	    return
328	
329	    # traces з»ҙеәҰдҫқе®һйҷ…иҖҢе®ҡпјҢеҸ–еқҮеҖјеҗҺжӢҝз¬¬ 0 дёӘ qubit зҡ„ж—¶й—ҙеәҸеҲ—
330	    # е…ёеһӢ shape: (repeat, shots, time, qubits) жҲ– (shots, time, qubits)
331	    tt = traces
332	    while tt.ndim > 2:
333	        tt = np.mean(tt, axis=0)   # йҖҗжӯҘеҜ№ repeat / shots иҪҙжұӮеқҮеҖј
334	    trace0 = tt[:, 0] if tt.ndim == 2 else tt   # еҸ– qubit 0
335	
336	    n_pts = len(trace0)
337	    # ADC йҮҮж ·зҺҮд»Һ NS_INST srate жҺЁз®—пјҢжҲ–й»ҳи®Өз”Ё 1 ns/зӮ№
338	    try:
339	        adc_sr = s.query('dev.NS_INST.srate')   # 6.4 GHz
340	        dt     = 1.0 / adc_sr
341	    except Exception:
342	        dt = 1e-9
343	    taxis = np.arange(n_pts) * dt * 1e9   # еҚ•дҪҚ ns
344	
345	    fig, axes = plt.subplots(2, 1, figsize=(9, 5), sharex=True)
346	    axes[0].plot(taxis, trace0.real, label='I')
347	    axes[0].set_ylabel('I (a.u.)'); axes[0].legend()
348	    axes[0].set_title(f'{QUBIT} ADC Trace  RID={task.rid}  TRIGD={trigd}s')
349	
350	    axes[1].plot(taxis, trace0.imag, label='Q', color='C1')
351	    axes[1].set_ylabel('Q (a.u.)'); axes[1].legend()
352	    axes[1].set_xlabel('Time (ns)')
353	
354	    # ж ҮеҮәеҪ“еүҚ weight зӘ—еҸЈ
355	    weight_str = s.query(f'{QUBIT}.Measure.weight')   # 'square(1800e-9)>>900e-9'
356	    try:
357	        import re
358	        m = re.search(r'square\((\S+)\)>>([\d.e+-]+)', weight_str)
359	        if m:
360	            w_len  = float(m.group(1)) * 1e9   # ns
361	            w_start = float(m.group(2)) * 1e9  # ns
362	            for ax in axes:
363	                ax.axvspan(w_start, w_start + w_len, alpha=0.15,
364	                           color='green', label='weight window')
365	    except Exception:
366	        pass
367	
368	    plt.tight_layout()
369	    savefig('00_trace')
370	
371	    # жүҫдҝЎеҸ·еҲ°иҫҫж—¶еҲ»пјҲI жҲ– Q е№…еәҰи¶…иҝҮжңҖеӨ§еҖј 10% зҡ„з¬¬дёҖдёӘзӮ№пјү
372	    amp = np.abs(trace0)
373	    threshold_arr = amp.max() * 0.1
374	    onset_idx = np.argmax(amp > threshold_arr)
375	    if onset_idx > 0:
376	        onset_ns = taxis[onset_idx]
377	        print(f'  и„үеҶІеҲ°иҫҫзәҰ {onset_ns:.1f} ns (зӮ№ {onset_idx})')
378	        print(f'  е»әи®®: иӢҘи„үеҶІеңЁзӘ—еҸЈеӨ–пјҢи°ғж•ҙ TRIGD жҲ– weight еҒҸз§»йҮҸ')
379	        print(f'  еҪ“еүҚ weight иө·е§Ӣ: {weight_str}')
380	    else:
381	        print('  жңӘжЈҖжөӢеҲ°жҳҺжҳҫдҝЎеҸ·пјҢиҜ·жҸҗй«ҳиҜ»еҮә amp еҗҺйҮҚиҜ•')
382	
383	    return traces
384	
385	
386	# в”Җв”Җв”Җ 1. S21 в”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җ
387	
388	def step_s21():
389	    print('\n' + '='*55)
390	    print('жӯҘйӘӨ 1 / S21 иҜ»еҮәи…”йҖҸе°„и°ұ')
391	    print('='*55)
392	
393	    center = s.query(f'{QUBIT}.Measure.frequency')
394	    print(f'  еҪ“еүҚи…”йў‘: {center/1e9:.6f} GHzпјҢжү«жҸҸ Вұ5 MHz')
395	
396	    rcp = Recipe('S21', signal='iq_avg')
397	    rcp.circuit = circuit_S21
398	    rcp['qubits'] = QUBITS
399	    rcp['freq'] = np.linspace(-5, 5, 201) * 1e6
400	    # rcp['freq'] = np.linspace(4, 8, 201)*1e9
401	    rcp[f'{QUBIT}.Measure.frequency'] = rcp['freq'] + center
402	    # rcp[f'{QUBIT}.Measure.amp'] = 0.3
403	    
404	    task = s.submit(rcp.export(), block=True, preview=[QUBIT], plot=False)
405	    task.bar()
406	    print(f'  RID = {task.rid}')
407	
408	    result = get_data_by_rid(task.rid)
409	    
410	    xaxis  = np.array(result['meta']['axis']['freq'][f'${QUBIT}.Measure.frequency'])
411	    iq     = np.array(result['data']['iq_avg'])[..., 0]
412	    amp    = np.abs(iq)
413	    print(amp)
414	    plt.plot(xaxis / 1e9, amp)
415	    savefig('01_s21_3')
416	    return
417	
418	    peaks, _ = find_peaks(-amp, prominence=0.003)
419	    fig, ax = plt.subplots(figsize=(7, 3))
420	    ax.plot(xaxis / 1e9, amp)
421	    for p in peaks:
422	        ax.plot(xaxis[p]/1e9, amp[p], 'ro')
423	        ax.annotate(f'{xaxis[p]/1e9:.5f} GHz',
424	                    (xaxis[p]/1e9, amp[p]), textcoords='offset points',
425	                    xytext=(4, 4), fontsize=8)
426	    ax.set_xlabel('Frequency (GHz)'); ax.set_ylabel('|IQ|')
427	    ax.set_title(f'{QUBIT} S21  RID={task.rid}')
428	    plt.tight_layout()
429	    savefig('01_S21')
430	    return
431	
432	    if len(peaks):
433	        readout_freq = float(xaxis[peaks[0]])
434	        print(f'  еҸ‘зҺ°и…”йў‘ = {readout_freq/1e9:.6f} GHz')
435	        s.update(f'{QUBIT}.Measure.frequency', readout_freq)
436	        print(f'  вң“ е·Іжӣҙж–° Measure.frequency')
437	        return readout_freq
438	    else:
439	        print('  вҡ  жңӘжүҫеҲ°еі°пјҢиҜ·жЈҖжҹҘжү«жҸҸиҢғеӣҙжҲ–иҜ»еҮә amp')
440	        return None
441	
442	
443	# в”Җв”Җв”Җ 2. Spectrum в”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җ
444	
445	def step_spectrum():    
446	    print('\n' + '='*55)
447	    print('жӯҘйӘӨ 2 / жҜ”зү№и·ғиҝҒи°ұ (Spectrum)')
448	    print('='*55)
449	
450	    rcp = Recipe('Spectrum', signal='iq_avg')
451	    rcp.circuit = circuit_Spectrum
452	    rcp['qubits'] = QUBITS
453	    rcp['repeat'] = np.arange(10)
454	    rcp['freq'] = np.linspace(3.8, 3.85, 101) * 1e9
455	    rcp[f'{QUBIT}.R.frequency'] = rcp['freq']
456	    rcp[f'{QUBIT}.R.amp']       = 1
457	    rcp[f'{QUBIT}.R.width']     = 2e-7
458	    print('  жү«жҸҸ 3.5 ~ 4.5 GHzпјҢжӯҘиҝӣ 1 MHzпјҢй©ұеҠЁ amp=0.8пјҢwidth=100 ns')
459	
460	    task = s.submit(rcp.export(), block=True, preview=['Q0'], plot=False)
461	    task.bar(interval=2)
462	    print(f'  RID = {task.rid}')
463	
464	    result = get_data_by_rid(task.rid)
465	    # result = get_data_by_rid(176)
466	    xaxis  = np.array(result['meta']['axis']['freq'][f'${QUBIT}.R.frequency'])
467	    iq = np.mean(np.array(result['data']['iq_avg'])[..., 0], axis=0)
468	    std = np.std(np.array(result['data']['iq_avg'])[..., 0], axis=0)
469	    amp    = np.abs(iq)
470	
471	    peaks, _ = find_peaks(amp, prominence=np.mean(std))
472	    fig, ax = plt.subplots(figsize=(8, 3))
473	    ax.plot(xaxis / 1e9, amp)
474	    ax.fill_between(xaxis/1e9, amp-std, amp+std, alpha=0.2)
475	    for p in peaks:
476	        ax.plot(xaxis[p]/1e9, amp[p], 'ro')
477	        ax.annotate(f'{xaxis[p]/1e9:.4f} GHz',
478	                    (xaxis[p]/1e9, amp[p]), textcoords='offset points',
479	                    xytext=(4, 4), fontsize=8)
480	    ax.set_xlabel('Frequency (GHz)'); ax.set_ylabel('|IQ|')
481	    ax.set_title(f'{QUBIT} Spectrum  RID={task.rid}')
482	    plt.tight_layout()
483	    savefig('02_Spectrum')
484	
485	    if len(peaks):
486	        qubit_freq = float(xaxis[peaks[0]])
487	        print(f'  f01 = {qubit_freq/1e9:.4f} GHz')
488	        s.update(f'{QUBIT}.R.frequency', qubit_freq)
489	        print(f'  вң“ е·Іжӣҙж–° R.frequency')
490	        return qubit_freq
491	    else:
492	        print('  вҡ  жңӘжүҫеҲ°еі°пјҢиҜ·и°ғж•ҙжү«жҸҸиҢғеӣҙжҲ–й©ұеҠЁеҸӮж•°')
493	        return None
494	
495	
496	# в”Җв”Җв”Җ 3. PowerRabi в”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җ
497	
498	def step_power_rabi():
499	    print('\n' + '='*55)
500	    print('жӯҘйӘӨ 3 / PowerRabi вҶ’ ПҖ и„үеҶІе№…еәҰ')
501	    print('='*55)
502	
503	    rcp = Recipe('PowerRabi', signal='iq_avg')
504	    rcp.circuit = circuit_Rabi
505	    rcp['qubits'] = QUBITS
506	    rcp['repeat'] = np.arange(10)
507	    rcp['amp'] = np.linspace(0, 1, 51)
508	    rcp[f'{QUBIT}.R.amp']   = rcp['amp']
509	    rcp[f'{QUBIT}.R.width'] = 100e-9
510	    print('  жү«жҸҸ amp 0вҶ’0.9пјҢwidth=100 ns')
511	
512	    task = s.submit(rcp.export(), block=True, preview=[QUBIT], plot=False)
513	    task.bar(interval=0.1)
514	    print(f'  RID = {task.rid}')
515	
516	    result = get_data_by_rid(task.rid)
517	    xaxis  = np.array(result['meta']['axis']['amp']['def'])
518	    iq = np.array(result['data']['iq_avg'])[..., 0]
519	    ydata  = np.abs(np.mean(iq, axis=0))
520	    std = np.std(iq, axis=0)
521	
522	    pi_amp = None
523	    fig, ax = plt.subplots(figsize=(6, 3))
524	    ax.plot(xaxis, ydata, 'o', ms=4, label='data')
525	    ax.fill_between(xaxis, ydata-std, ydata+std, alpha=0.2)
526	    try:
527	        (A, f, phi, B), x_fit, y_fit = fit_Rabi(xaxis, ydata)
528	        pi_amp = 0.5 / f
529	        ax.plot(x_fit, y_fit, '-', label=f'fit  ПҖ_amp={pi_amp:.4f}')
530	        ax.axvline(pi_amp, color='r', ls='--')
531	        print(f'  ПҖ amp = {pi_amp:.4f}')
532	    except Exception as e:
533	        print(f'  вҡ  жӢҹеҗҲеӨұиҙҘ: {e}')
534	    ax.set_xlabel('Drive amp'); ax.set_ylabel('Population |1вҹ©')
535	    ax.set_title(f'{QUBIT} PowerRabi  RID={task.rid}'); ax.legend()
536	    plt.tight_layout()
537	    savefig('03_PowerRabi')
538	
539	    if pi_amp:
540	        # s.update(f'{QUBIT}.R.amp', pi_amp)
541	        print(f'  вң“ е·Іжӣҙж–° R.amp = {pi_amp:.4f}')
542	    return pi_amp
543	
544	
545	# в”Җв”Җв”Җ 4. TimeRabi в”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җ
546	
547	def step_time_rabi():
548	    print('\n' + '='*55)
549	    print('жӯҘйӘӨ 4 / TimeRabi вҶ’ ПҖ и„үеҶІж—¶й•ҝ')
550	    print('='*55)
551	
552	    current_amp = s.query(f'{QUBIT}.R.amp')
553	    print(f'  дҪҝз”ЁеҪ“еүҚ R.amp = {current_amp:.4f}пјҢжү«жҸҸ width 0вҶ’200 ns')
554	
555	    rcp = Recipe('TimeRabi', signal='iq_avg')
556	    rcp.circuit = circuit_time_Rabi
557	    rcp['qubits'] = QUBITS
558	    rcp['repeat'] = np.arange(20)
559	    rcp['duration'] = np.linspace(0, 500, 51) * 1e-9
560	    rcp[f'{QUBIT}.R.width'] = 5e-9
561	    rcp[f'{QUBIT}.R.amp']   = 1
562	
563	    task = s.submit(rcp.export(), block=True, preview=[QUBIT], plot=False)
564	    task.bar(interval=0.5)
565	    print(f'  RID = {task.rid}')
566	
567	    result = get_data_by_rid(task.rid)
568	    xaxis  = np.array(result['meta']['axis']['duration']['def'])
569	    iq  = np.mean(np.array(result['data']['iq_avg'])[..., 0], axis=0)
570	    std  = np.std(np.array(result['data']['iq_avg'])[..., 0], axis=0)
571	    ydata = np.abs(iq)
572	
573	    pi_width = None
574	    fig, ax = plt.subplots(figsize=(6, 3))
575	    ax.plot(xaxis * 1e9, ydata, 'o', ms=4, label='data')
576	    ax.fill_between(xaxis * 1e9, ydata-std, ydata+std, alpha=0.2)
577	    try:
578	        (A, f, phi, B), x_fit, y_fit = fit_Rabi(xaxis, ydata)
579	        pi_width = 0.5 / f
580	        ax.plot(x_fit * 1e9, y_fit, '-', label=f'fit  ПҖ_width={pi_width*1e9:.1f}ns')
581	        ax.axvline(pi_width * 1e9, color='r', ls='--')
582	        print(f'  ПҖ width = {pi_width*1e9:.2f} ns')
583	    except Exception as e:
584	        print(f'  вҡ  жӢҹеҗҲеӨұиҙҘ: {e}')
585	    ax.set_xlabel('Width (ns)'); ax.set_ylabel('Population |1вҹ©')
586	    ax.set_title(f'{QUBIT} TimeRabi  RID={task.rid}'); ax.legend()
587	    plt.tight_layout()
588	    savefig('04_TimeRabi')
589	
590	    if pi_width:
591	        #s.update(f'{QUBIT}.R.width', pi_width)
592	        print(f'  вң“ е·Іжӣҙж–° R.width = {pi_width*1e9:.2f} ns')
593	    return pi_width
594	
595	
596	# в”Җв”Җв”Җ 5. SingleShot в”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җ
597	
598	def step_single_shot():
599	    print('\n' + '='*55)
600	    print('жӯҘйӘӨ 5 / SingleShot иҜ»еҮәж ЎеҮҶ')
601	    print('='*55)
602	
603	    rcp = Recipe('SingleShot', signal='iq')
604	    rcp.circuit = circuit_SingleShot
605	    rcp['qubits'] = QUBITS
606	    rcp['repeat'] = list(range(1000))
607	    rcp['state']  = [0, 1]
608	    print('  state=[0,1], repeat=4  вҶ’  жҜҸжҖҒ ~4096 shots')
609	
610	    task = s.submit(rcp.export(), block=True, preview=[QUBIT], plot=False)
611	    task.bar(interval=0.1)
612	    print(f'  RID = {task.rid}')
613	
614	    result = get_data_by_rid(task.rid)
615	    # result = get_data_by_rid(237)
616	    qubits = result['meta']['other']['qubits']
617	    data   = np.array(result['data']['iq'])
618	    s0, s1 = data[:, 0, :, 0], data[:, 1, :, 0]
619	    # s0, s1 = s0.reshape(-1), s1.reshape(-1)
620	    s0, s1 = np.mean(s0, axis=1), np.mean(s1, axis=1)
621	
622	    from wath import get_threshold_info
623	    info = get_threshold_info(s0, s1)
624	    threshold = info['threshold']
625	    phi       = info['phi']
626	    vis, Pg, Pe = info['visibility']
627	    PgPe = [1 - Pg, 1 - Pe]
628	
629	    print(f'  threshold = {threshold:.5f}')
630	    print(f'  phi       = {phi:.5f} rad')
631	    print(f'  visibility= {vis:.3f}')
632	    print(f'  F_g(|0вҹ©)  = {Pg:.3f}   F_e(|1вҹ©) = {1-Pe:.3f}')
633	
634	    from matplotlib.patches import Circle
635	    fig, axes = plt.subplots(1, 2, figsize=(9, 4))
636	    ax1, ax2 = axes
637	    ax1.plot(s0.real, s0.imag, '.', alpha=0.2, ms=2, label='|0вҹ©')
638	    ax1.plot(s1.real, s1.imag, '.', alpha=0.2, ms=2, label='|1вҹ©')
639	
640	    xi, yi = np.mean(s0).real, np.mean(s0).imag
641	    ri = np.std(s0)
642	    ax1.plot(xi, yi, 'o', color='C0')
643	    circle = Circle((xi, yi), ri, fill=False, alpha=0.5, color='C0')  # еҸҜиҮӘе®ҡд№үйўңиүІ
644	    ax1.add_patch(circle)
645	    xi, yi = np.mean(s1).real, np.mean(s1).imag
646	    ri = np.std(s1)
647	    ax1.plot(xi, yi, 'o', color='C1')
648	    circle = Circle((xi, yi), ri, fill=False, alpha=0.5, color='C1')  # еҸҜиҮӘе®ҡд№үйўңиүІ
649	    ax1.add_patch(circle)
650	
651	    ax1.set_xlabel('I'); ax1.set_ylabel('Q')
652	    ax1.axis("equal")
653	    ax1.legend(); ax1.set_title(f'{QUBIT} IQ scatter')
654	    s0r = (s0 * np.exp(-1j * phi)).real
655	    s1r = (s1 * np.exp(-1j * phi)).real
656	    bins = np.linspace(min(s0r.min(), s1r.min()),
657	                       max(s0r.max(), s1r.max()), 80)
658	    ax2.hist(s0r, bins=bins, alpha=0.6, label='|0вҹ©')
659	    ax2.hist(s1r, bins=bins, alpha=0.6, label='|1вҹ©')
660	    ax2.axvline(threshold, color='r', ls='--', label=f'thr={threshold:.4f}')
661	    ax2.set_title(f'F_g={Pg:.3f}  F_e={1-Pe:.3f}  vis={vis:.3f}')
662	    ax2.legend()
663	    plt.tight_layout()
664	    savefig('05_SingleShot')
665	
666	    s.update(f'{QUBIT}.Measure.threshold', threshold)
667	    s.update(f'{QUBIT}.Measure.phi',       phi)
668	    s.update(f'{QUBIT}.Measure.PgPe',      PgPe)
669	    print('  вң“ threshold / phi / PgPe е·Іжӣҙж–°')
670	    return threshold, phi, PgPe
671	
672	
673	# в”Җв”Җв”Җ 6. Ramsey в”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җ
674	
675	def step_ramsey():
676	    print('\n' + '='*55)
677	    print('жӯҘйӘӨ 6 / Ramsey вҶ’ T2* + йў‘зҺҮзІҫж Ў')
678	    print('='*55)
679	
680	
681	    rcp = Recipe('Ramsey', signal='iq_avg')
682	    rcp.circuit = circuit_Ramsey
683	    rcp['qubits'] = QUBITS
684	    rcp['repeat'] = np.arange(100)
685	    rcp['phase'] = np.linspace(0, 2*np.pi, 3, endpoint=False)
686	    rcp['delay']  = np.linspace(0, 1, 201) * 1e-6
687	
688	    task = s.submit(rcp.export(), block=True, preview=[QUBIT], plot=False)
689	    task.bar(interval=2)
690	    print(f'  RID = {task.rid}')
691	
692	    result = get_data_by_rid(task.rid)
693	    xaxis  = np.array(result['meta']['axis']['delay']['def'])
694	    iq = np.array(result['data']['iq_avg'])[..., 0]
695	    ydata  = np.abs(np.mean(iq, axis=0))
696	
697	    T2star = delta = new_freq = None
698	    
699	    from wath import fit_cosine
700	    R, offset, phi = fit_cosine(ydata)
701	    fig, ax = plt.subplots(figsize=(8, 3))
702	    ax.plot(xaxis * 1e6, ydata.T, 'o', ms=3, label='data')
703	    ax.fill_between(xaxis * 1e6, -R+offset, R+offset, alpha=0.2)
704	    # try:
705	    #     popt, x_fit, y_fit = fit_Ramsey(xdata=xaxis, ydata=ydata, T1=500e-6)
706	    #     A, T2star, Delta, phi, B = popt
707	    #     delta    = Delta - ROTATE
708	    #     ori_freq = get_config_by_rid(task.rid)[QUBIT]['R']['frequency']
709	    #     new_freq = ori_freq + delta
710	    #     ax.plot(x_fit * 1e6, y_fit, '-',
711	    #             label=f'T2*={T2star*1e6:.2f}Ојs  О”f={delta/1e3:.1f}kHz')
712	    #     print(f'  T2* = {T2star*1e6:.2f} Ојs')
713	    #     print(f'  О”f  = {delta/1e3:.1f} kHz  вҶ’  f01 = {new_freq/1e9:.6f} GHz')
714	    # except Exception as e:
715	    #     print(f'  вҡ  жӢҹеҗҲеӨұиҙҘ: {e}')
716	    ax.set_xlabel('Delay (Ојs)'); ax.set_ylabel('Population |1вҹ©')
717	    ax.set_title(f'{QUBIT} Ramsey  RID={task.rid}'); ax.legend()
718	    plt.tight_layout()
719	    savefig('06_Ramsey')
720	
721	    # if new_freq:
722	    #     s.update(f'{QUBIT}.R.frequency', new_freq)
723	    #     print(f'  вң“ е·Іжӣҙж–° R.frequency = {new_freq/1e9:.6f} GHz')
724	    # if T2star:
725	    #     s.update(f'{QUBIT}.params.T2_star', T2star)
726	    #     print(f'  вң“ е·Іи®°еҪ• T2* = {T2star*1e6:.2f} Ојs')
727	    # return T2star, delta
728

730	# в”Җв”Җв”Җ 7. T1 в”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җ
731	
732	def step_t1():
733	    print('\n' + '='*55)
734	    print('жӯҘйӘӨ 7 / T1 иғҪйҮҸејӣиұ«')
735	    print('='*55)
736	    print('  delay еҜ№ж•°жү«жҸҸ 1 ns вҶ’ 1 ms (51зӮ№)')
737	
738	    rcp = Recipe('T1', signal='iq_avg')
739	    rcp.circuit = circuit_T1
740	    rcp['qubits'] = QUBITS
741	    tlist = np.logspace(-2, 2, 41) * 1e-6
742	    # tlist = np.linspace(0, 1e-6, 51)
743	    rcp['repeat'] = np.arange(100)
744	    rcp['state'] = [0, 1]
745	    rcp['delay']  = tlist[tlist <= 90e-6]
746	
747	    task = s.submit(rcp.export(), block=True, preview=[QUBIT], plot=False)
748	    task.bar(interval=2)
749	    print(f'  RID = {task.rid}')
750	
751	    result = get_data_by_rid(task.rid)
752	    xaxis  = np.array(result['meta']['axis']['delay']['def'])
753	    iq   = np.array(result['data']['iq_avg'])
754	    ydata  = np.abs(np.mean(iq[..., 0], axis=0))
755	    std = np.std(iq[..., 0], axis=0)
756	
757	    T1_val = None
758	    fig, ax = plt.subplots(figsize=(6, 3))
759	    ax.plot(xaxis * 1e6, ydata[0], 'o', color='C0', ms=4, label='data')
760	    ax.fill_between(xaxis * 1e6, ydata[0]-std[0], ydata[0]+std[0], color='C0', alpha=0.2)
761	
762	    ax.plot(xaxis * 1e6, ydata[1], 'o', color='C1', ms=4, label='data')
763	    ax.fill_between(xaxis * 1e6, ydata[1]-std[1], ydata[1]+std[1], color='C1', alpha=0.2)
764	    try:
765	        (A, T1_val, B), y_fit = fit_T1(xaxis, ydata)
766	        ax.plot(xaxis * 1e6, y_fit, '-', color='C1', label=f'T1={T1_val*1e6:.2f}Ојs')
767	        ax.axhline(B, color='C0')
768	        print(f'  T1 = {T1_val*1e6:.2f} Ојs')
769	    except Exception as e:
770	        print(f'  вҡ  жӢҹеҗҲеӨұиҙҘ: {e}')
771	    ax.set_xscale('log')
772	    ax.set_xlabel('Delay (Ојs)'); ax.set_ylabel('Population |1вҹ©')
773	    ax.set_title(f'{QUBIT} T1  RID={task.rid}'); ax.legend()
774	    plt.tight_layout()
775	    savefig('07_T1')
776	
777	    if T1_val:
778	        s.update(f'{QUBIT}.params.T1', T1_val)
779	        print(f'  вң“ е·Іи®°еҪ• T1 = {T1_val*1e6:.2f} Ојs')
780	    return T1_val
781	
782	
783	# в”Җв”Җв”Җ 8. R12 в”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җ
784	
785	def step_r12():
786	    print('\n' + '='*55)
787	    print('жӯҘйӘӨ 8 / R12 и·ғиҝҒи°ұ + ПҖ12 и„үеҶІж ЎеҮҶ')
788	    print('='*55)
789	
790	    f01 = s.query(f'{QUBIT}.R.frequency')
791	
792	    # 8a. Spectrum12
793	    print('  [8a] Spectrum12 жү«жҸҸ f01-400 MHz ~ f01+50 MHz')
794	    rcp = Recipe('Spectrum12', signal='population')
795	    rcp.circuit = circuit_R12
796	    rcp['qubits'] = QUBITS
797	    rcp['freq'] = np.linspace(-400, 50, 251) * 1e6
798	    rcp[f'{QUBIT}.R12.frequency'] = rcp['freq'] + f01
799	    rcp[f'{QUBIT}.R12.amp']   = 0.05
800	    rcp[f'{QUBIT}.R12.width'] = 1.6e-7
801	
802	    task = s.submit(rcp.export(), block=True, preview=[], plot=False)
803	    task.bar(interval=2)
804	    print(f'  RID = {task.rid}')
805	
806	    result = get_data_by_rid(task.rid)
807	    xaxis  = np.array(result['meta']['axis']['freq'][f'${QUBIT}.R12.frequency'])
808	    ydata  = np.abs(np.array(result['data']['population'])[:, 0])
809	    peaks, _ = find_peaks(ydata, prominence=0.01)
810	
811	    fig, ax = plt.subplots(figsize=(8, 3))
812	    ax.plot(xaxis / 1e9, ydata)
813	    f12 = None
814	    if len(peaks):
815	        f12 = float(xaxis[peaks[0]])
816	        ax.axvline(f12/1e9, color='r', ls='--', label=f'f12={f12/1e9:.4f} GHz')
817	        anharmonicity = f12 - f01
818	        print(f'  f12 = {f12/1e9:.4f} GHz')
819	        print(f'  йқһи°җжҖ§ Оұ = {anharmonicity/1e6:.1f} MHz')
820	    else:
821	        print('  вҡ  жңӘжүҫеҲ° f12пјҢиҜ·и°ғж•ҙжү«жҸҸиҢғеӣҙ')
822	    ax.set_xlabel('Frequency (GHz)'); ax.set_ylabel('Population')
823	    ax.set_title(f'{QUBIT} R12 Spectrum  RID={task.rid}'); ax.legend()
824	    plt.tight_layout()
825	    savefig('08a_Spectrum12')
826	
827	    if f12:
828	        s.update(f'{QUBIT}.R12.frequency', f12)
829	        print(f'  вң“ е·Іжӣҙж–° R12.frequency = {f12/1e9:.4f} GHz')
830	
831	    # 8b. PowerRabi12
832	    print('  [8b] PowerRabi12 жү«жҸҸ amp 0вҶ’0.3')
833	    rcp2 = Recipe('PowerRabi12', signal='population')
834	    rcp2.circuit = circuit_R12
835	    rcp2['qubits'] = QUBITS
836	    rcp2['amp'] = np.linspace(0, 0.3, 51)
837	    rcp2[f'{QUBIT}.R12.amp'] = rcp2['amp']
838	
839	    task2 = s.submit(rcp2.export(), block=True, preview=[], plot=False)
840	    task2.bar(interval=0.5)
841	    print(f'  RID = {task2.rid}')
842	
843	    result2 = get_data_by_rid(task2.rid)
844	    xaxis2  = np.array(result2['meta']['axis']['amp']['def'])
845	    ydata2  = np.abs(np.array(result2['data']['population'])[:, 0])
846	
847	    pi12_amp = None
848	    fig, ax = plt.subplots(figsize=(6, 3))
849	    ax.plot(xaxis2, ydata2, 'o', ms=4, label='data')
850	    try:
851	        (A, f, phi, B), x_fit, y_fit = fit_Rabi(xaxis2, ydata2)
852	        pi12_amp = 0.5 / f
853	        ax.plot(x_fit, y_fit, '-', label=f'ПҖ12_amp={pi12_amp:.4f}')
854	        ax.axvline(pi12_amp, color='r', ls='--')
855	        print(f'  ПҖ12 amp = {pi12_amp:.4f}')
856	    except Exception as e:
857	        print(f'  вҡ  жӢҹеҗҲеӨұиҙҘ: {e}')
858	    ax.set_xlabel('R12 amp'); ax.set_ylabel('Population')
859	    ax.set_title(f'{QUBIT} PowerRabi12  RID={task2.rid}'); ax.legend()
860	    plt.tight_layout()
861	    savefig('08b_PowerRabi12')
862	
863	    if pi12_amp:
864	        s.update(f'{QUBIT}.R12.amp', pi12_amp)
865	        print(f'  вң“ е·Іжӣҙж–° R12.amp = {pi12_amp:.4f}')
866	    return f12, pi12_amp
867	
868	
869	# в”Җв”Җв”Җ 9b. S21 @ fixed amp вҶ’ ReadoutSNR в”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җ
870	
871	def step_s21_readout_snr(probe_amp=0.3):
872	    """е…ҲеңЁжҢҮе®ҡ amp дёӢжү« S21 е®ҡи…”йў‘пјҢеҶҚд»ҘжӯӨдёәдёӯеҝғи·‘ 2D readout SNR дјҳеҢ–гҖӮ"""
873	    print('\n' + '='*55)
874	    print(f'жӯҘйӘӨ 9b / S21 @ amp={probe_amp}  вҶ’  ReadoutSNR')
875	    print('='*55)
876	
877	    # в”Җв”Җ [1/2] S21 в”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җ
878	    center = s.query(f'{QUBIT}.Measure.frequency')
879	    print(f'\n[1/2] S21 @ amp={probe_amp}  дёӯеҝғ: {center/1e9:.6f} GHz  Вұ5 MHz')
880	
881	    rcp = Recipe('S21_probe', signal='iq_avg')
882	    rcp.circuit = circuit_S21
883	    rcp['qubits'] = QUBITS
884	    rcp['freq'] = np.linspace(-5, 5, 201) * 1e6
885	    rcp[f'{QUBIT}.Measure.frequency'] = rcp['freq'] + center
886	    rcp[f'{QUBIT}.Measure.amp'] = probe_amp
887	
888	    task = s.submit(rcp.export(), block=True, preview=[], plot=False)
889	    task.bar(interval=0.1)
890	    print(f'  RID = {task.rid}')
891	
892	    result = get_data_by_rid(task.rid)
893	    xaxis = np.array(result['meta']['axis']['freq'][f'${QUBIT}.Measure.frequency'])
894	    s21   = np.abs(np.array(result['data']['iq_avg'])[..., 0])
895	
896	    # жүҫи…”йў‘пјҡS21 йҖҸе°„и°·пјҲdipпјү
897	    peaks, props = find_peaks(-s21, prominence=np.std(s21) * 0.3)
898	    if len(peaks):
899	        best_peak = peaks[np.argmax(props['prominences'])]
900	        cavity_freq = float(xaxis[best_peak])
901	        print(f'  жүҫеҲ°йҖҸе°„и°·: {cavity_freq/1e9:.6f} GHz')
902	    else:
903	        cavity_freq = float(xaxis[np.argmin(s21)])
904	        print(f'  жңӘжүҫеҲ°жҳҺжҳҫи°·пјҢеҸ–е№…еәҰжңҖе°ҸзӮ№: {cavity_freq/1e9:.6f} GHz')
905	
906	    fig, ax = plt.subplots(figsize=(7, 3))
907	    ax.plot(xaxis / 1e9, s21)
908	    ax.axvline(cavity_freq / 1e9, color='r', ls='--',
909	               label=f'{cavity_freq/1e9:.5f} GHz')
910	    ax.set_xlabel('Frequency (GHz)'); ax.set_ylabel('|IQ| (a.u.)')
911	    ax.set_title(f'{QUBIT} S21 @ amp={probe_amp}  RID={task.rid}')
912	    ax.legend(); plt.tight_layout()
913	    savefig('09b_S21_probe')
914	
915	    # в”Җв”Җ [2/2] ReadoutSNR centered on cavity_freq в”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җ
916	    print(f'\n[2/2] ReadoutSNR  дёӯеҝғ: {cavity_freq/1e9:.6f} GHz')
917	    s.update(f'{QUBIT}.Measure.frequency', cavity_freq)
918	    step_readout_snr()
919	
920	
921	# в”Җв”Җв”Җ 9. ReadoutSNR в”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җ
922	
923	def step_readout_snr():
924	    """2D иҜ»еҮәеҸӮж•°дјҳеҢ–пјҡжү«жҸҸиҜ»еҮәйў‘зҺҮ Г— е№…еәҰпјҢжңҖеӨ§еҢ– IQ дҝЎеҷӘжҜ”гҖӮ
925	
926	    дҝЎеҸ· = |ОјвӮҒ - ОјвӮҖ|  пјҲдёӨжҖҒ IQ еқҮеҖјеңЁеӨҚж•°е№ійқўдёҠзҡ„и·қзҰ»пјү
927	    еҷӘеЈ° = (ПғвӮҖ + ПғвӮҒ) / 2  пјҲдёӨжҖҒеҚ•ж¬Ў IQ ж ҮеҮҶе·®зҡ„е№іеқҮпјү
928	    SNR  = дҝЎеҸ· / еҷӘеЈ°
929	    """
930	    print('\n' + '='*55)
931	    print('жӯҘйӘӨ 9 / иҜ»еҮә SNR дјҳеҢ– (йў‘зҺҮ Г— е№…еәҰ 2D жү«жҸҸ)')
932	    print('='*55)
933	
934	    center_freq = s.query(f'{QUBIT}.Measure.frequency')
935	    center_amp  = s.query(f'{QUBIT}.Measure.amp')
936	    print(f'  еҪ“еүҚиҜ»еҮәйў‘зҺҮ: {center_freq/1e9:.6f} GHz')
937	    print(f'  еҪ“еүҚиҜ»еҮәе№…еәҰ: {center_amp:.4f}')
938	
939	    # в”Җв”Җ жү«жҸҸиҢғеӣҙ в”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җ
940	    freq_span = 10e6           # Вұ3 MHz
941	    n_freq    = 101
942	    amp_min, amp_max = 0.02, 1.0
943	    n_amp     = 101
944	
945	    freq_array = np.linspace(center_freq - freq_span / 2,
946	                             center_freq + freq_span / 2, n_freq)
947	    amp_array  = np.linspace(amp_min, amp_max, n_amp)
948	    print(f'  йў‘зҺҮиҢғеӣҙ: {freq_array[0]/1e9:.4f} ~ {freq_array[-1]/1e9:.4f} GHz  ({n_freq} pts)')
949	    print(f'  е№…еәҰиҢғеӣҙ: {amp_min:.3f} ~ {amp_max:.3f}  ({n_amp} pts)')
950	    print(f'  жҖ»з”өи·Ҝж•°: {n_freq * n_amp * 2}  (Г—1024 shots/ж¬Ў)')
951	
952	    # в”Җв”Җ жҸҗдәӨе®һйӘҢ в”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җ
953	    rcp = Recipe('ReadoutSNR', signal='iq')
954	    rcp.circuit = circuit_SingleShot
955	    rcp['qubits'] = QUBITS
956	    rcp['state']  = [0, 1]
957	    rcp['freq']   = freq_array
958	    rcp['amp']    = amp_array
959	    rcp[f'{QUBIT}.Measure.frequency'] = rcp['freq']
960	    rcp[f'{QUBIT}.Measure.amp']       = rcp['amp']
961	
962	    task = s.submit(rcp.export(), block=True, preview=[], plot=False)
963	    task.bar(interval=1)
964	    print(f'  RID = {task.rid}')
965	
966	    if task.status()['status'] == 'Failed':
967	        print('  вң— д»»еҠЎеӨұиҙҘпјҢиҜ·жЈҖжҹҘ server ж—Ҙеҝ—')
968	        return None
969	
970	    # в”Җв”Җ и§Јжһҗж•°жҚ® в”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җ
971	    result = get_data_by_rid(task.rid)
972	    data   = np.array(result['data']['iq'])
973	    # жңҹжңӣ shape: (n_state, n_freq, n_amp, n_shots, n_qubits)
974	    print(f'  data shape = {data.shape}')
975	
976	    iq = data[..., 0]                       # вҶ’ (n_state, n_freq, n_amp, n_shots)
977	    mean_iq = np.mean(iq, axis=-1)          # вҶ’ (n_state, n_freq, n_amp)  еӨҚж•°еқҮеҖј
978	    std_iq  = np.std(iq,  axis=-1)          # вҶ’ (n_state, n_freq, n_amp)  е®һж•°ж ҮеҮҶе·®пјҲ|IQ| spreadпјү
979	
980	    mean_0, mean_1 = mean_iq[0], mean_iq[1]
981	    std_0,  std_1  = std_iq[0],  std_iq[1]
982	
983	    # в”Җв”Җ и®Ўз®— SNR в”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җ
984	    signal_2d = np.abs(mean_1 - mean_0)            # (n_freq, n_amp)
985	    noise_2d  = (std_0 + std_1) / 2                # (n_freq, n_amp)
986	    snr_2d    = signal_2d / (noise_2d + 1e-12)     # (n_freq, n_amp)
987	
988	    # в”Җв”Җ жүҫжңҖдјҳеҸӮж•° в”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җ
989	    idx_flat  = np.argmax(snr_2d)
990	    idx       = np.unravel_index(idx_flat, snr_2d.shape)
991	    best_freq = float(freq_array[idx[0]])
992	    best_amp  = float(amp_array[idx[1]])
993	    best_snr  = float(snr_2d[idx])
994	
995	    print(f'  жңҖдјҳиҜ»еҮәйў‘зҺҮ: {best_freq/1e9:.6f} GHz  (еҺҹ: {center_freq/1e9:.6f})')
996	    print(f'  жңҖдјҳиҜ»еҮәе№…еәҰ: {best_amp:.4f}  (еҺҹ: {center_amp:.4f})')
997	    print(f'  жңҖеӨ§ SNR:     {best_snr:.3f}')
998	    fi0 = np.argmin(np.abs(freq_array - center_freq))
999	    ai0 = np.argmin(np.abs(amp_array  - center_amp))
1000	    snr0 = float(snr_2d[fi0, ai0])
1001	    print(f'  еҺҹеҸӮж•° SNR:   {snr0:.3f}  (freq idx={fi0}, amp idx={ai0})')
1002	
1003	    # в”Җв”Җ з»ҳеӣҫ в”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җ
1004	    freq_ghz = freq_array / 1e9
1005	    # imshow extent: [xmin, xmax, ymin, ymax] with x=amp, y=freq
1006	    extent = [amp_array[0], amp_array[-1], freq_ghz[0], freq_ghz[-1]]
1007	
1008	    fig, axes = plt.subplots(2, 3, figsize=(15, 9))
1009	
1010	    def _imshow(ax, z, title, cmap='viridis'):
1011	        im = ax.imshow(z, origin='lower', aspect='auto', extent=extent, cmap=cmap)
1012	        ax.plot(best_amp, best_freq / 1e9, 'r*', ms=12, label=f'best SNR={best_snr:.2f}')
1013	        ax.set_xlabel('Amplitude'); ax.set_ylabel('Frequency (GHz)')
1014	        ax.set_title(title); ax.legend(fontsize=8)
1015	        plt.colorbar(im, ax=ax)
1016	
1017	    _imshow(axes[0, 0], snr_2d,    'SNR = signal / noise')
1018	    _imshow(axes[0, 1], signal_2d, 'Signal  |u1 - u0|  (a.u.)', 'plasma')
1019	    _imshow(axes[0, 2], noise_2d,  'Noise  (s0+s1)/2  (a.u.)', 'inferno')
1020	
1021	    # freq slice at best amp
1022	    ax = axes[1, 0]
1023	    ax.plot(freq_ghz, snr_2d[:, idx[1]], 'o-', ms=4)
1024	    ax.axvline(best_freq / 1e9, color='r', ls='--',
1025	               label=f'best {best_freq/1e9:.4f} GHz')
1026	    ax.set_xlabel('Frequency (GHz)'); ax.set_ylabel('SNR')
1027	    ax.set_title(f'Freq slice @ amp={best_amp:.3f}'); ax.legend()
1028	
1029	    # amp slice at best freq
1030	    ax = axes[1, 1]
1031	    ax.plot(amp_array, snr_2d[idx[0], :], 'o-', ms=4)
1032	    ax.axvline(best_amp, color='r', ls='--',
1033	               label=f'best amp={best_amp:.3f}')
1034	    ax.set_xlabel('Amplitude'); ax.set_ylabel('SNR')
1035	    ax.set_title(f'Amp slice @ {best_freq/1e9:.4f} GHz'); ax.legend()
1036	
1037	    # IQ scatter at best params
1038	    ax = axes[1, 2]
1039	    shots_0 = iq[0, idx[0], idx[1], :]     # (n_shots,) complex
1040	    shots_1 = iq[1, idx[0], idx[1], :]
1041	    ax.plot(shots_0.real, shots_0.imag, '.', alpha=0.3, ms=2, label='|0>')
1042	    ax.plot(shots_1.real, shots_1.imag, '.', alpha=0.3, ms=2, label='|1>')
1043	    ax.plot(mean_0[idx[0], idx[1]].real, mean_0[idx[0], idx[1]].imag,
1044	            'o', ms=8, color='C0', zorder=5)
1045	    ax.plot(mean_1[idx[0], idx[1]].real, mean_1[idx[0], idx[1]].imag,
1046	            'o', ms=8, color='C1', zorder=5)
1047	    ax.set_xlabel('I'); ax.set_ylabel('Q')
1048	    ax.set_title(f'IQ scatter @ best params  SNR={best_snr:.2f}')
1049	    ax.axis('equal'); ax.legend()
1050	
1051	    plt.suptitle(
1052	        f'{QUBIT} Readout SNR optimization  RID={task.rid}  '
1053	        f'best: f={best_freq/1e9:.4f} GHz  amp={best_amp:.3f}',
1054	        fontsize=11)
1055	    plt.tight_layout()
1056	    savefig('09_ReadoutSNR')
1057	
1058	    # в”Җв”Җ жӣҙж–°еҸӮж•° в”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җ
1059	    s.update(f'{QUBIT}.Measure.frequency', best_freq)
1060	    s.update(f'{QUBIT}.Measure.amp',       best_amp)
1061	    print('  вң“ Measure.frequency / Measure.amp е·Іжӣҙж–°')
1062	
1063	    return best_freq, best_amp, snr_2d
1064	
1065	
1066	# в”Җв”Җв”Җ 10. Summary в”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җ
1067	
1068	def step_summary():
1069	    print('\n' + '='*55)
1070	    print(f'иЎЁеҫҒз»“жһңжұҮжҖ»  ж ·е“Ғ={s.query("station.sample")}  жҜ”зү№={QUBIT}')
1071	    print('='*55)
1072	    rows = [
1073	        ('Measure.frequency', 'иҜ»еҮәи…”йў‘зҺҮ', 'GHz',  1e9),
1074	        ('R.frequency',       'f01',        'GHz',  1e9),
1075	        ('R12.frequency',     'f12',        'GHz',  1e9),
1076	        ('R.amp',             'ПҖ amp',      '',     1),
1077	        ('R.width',           'ПҖ width',    'ns',   1e-9),
1078	        ('R12.amp',           'ПҖ12 amp',    '',     1),
1079	        ('Measure.threshold', 'threshold',  '',     1),
1080	        ('Measure.phi',       'ПҶ',          'rad',  1),
1081	        ('Measure.PgPe',      'PgPe',       '',     1),
1082	        ('params.T1',         'T1',         'Ојs',   1e-6),
1083	        ('params.T2_star',    'T2*',        'Ојs',   1e-6),
1084	    ]
1085	    for key, label, unit, scale in rows:
1086	        val = s.query(f'{QUBIT}.{key}')
1087	        if scale not in (1, None) and isinstance(val, (int, float)):
1088	            print(f'  {label:20s} = {val/scale:.4f} {unit}')
1089	        else:
1090	            print(f'  {label:20s} = {val} {unit}')
1091	    print('='*55)
1092

1094	# в”Җв”Җв”Җ S0. debug в”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җ
1095	
1096	def step_debug():
1097	    from matplotlib.patches import Circle
1098	
1099	    cmap = plt.get_cmap('coolwarm')
1100	    rcp = Recipe('debug', signal='iq')
1101	    rcp.circuit = circuit_delay_readout
1102	    rcp['qubits'] = QUBITS
1103	    rcp['repeat'] = np.arange(10)
1104	    # tlist = np.logspace(-3, 2, 51) * 1e-6
1105	    tlist = np.linspace(0, 3e-6, 31)
1106	    # tlist = np.arange(100)*16e-9
1107	    # tlist = np.ones(100)*16e-9
1108	    # tlist = np.hstack([np.linspace(0, 8e-9, 33), np.linspace(0, 8e-9, 33)+100e-9])
1109	    rcp['delay']  = tlist[tlist <= 90e-6]
1110	
1111	    task = s.submit(rcp.export(), block=True, preview=['Q0'], plot=False)
1112	    task.bar(interval=2)
1113	    print(f'  RID = {task.rid}')
1114	
1115	    result = get_data_by_rid(task.rid)
1116	    xaxis  = np.array(result['meta']['axis']['delay']['def'])
1117	    data   = np.array(result['data']['iq'])
1118	    iq_avg = np.mean(data[..., 0], axis=-1)
1119	    iq_std = 1#np.mean(np.std(data[..., 0], axis=-1))
1120	    iq = np.mean(iq_avg, axis=0)/iq_std
1121	    x, y = iq.real, iq.imag
1122	    r = np.std(iq_avg, axis=0)/iq_std
1123	    
1124	    fig, ax = plt.subplots(figsize=(6, 6))
1125	    for index, (xi, yi, ri) in enumerate(zip(x, y, r)):
1126	        circle = Circle((xi, yi), ri, fill=False, alpha=0.5, color=cmap(index/len(x)))  # еҸҜиҮӘе®ҡд№үйўңиүІ
1127	        ax.add_patch(circle)
1128	    ax.plot(x, y, '-k', ms=4)
1129	    for index, (xi, yi, ri) in enumerate(zip(x, y, r)):
1130	        color = cmap(index/len(x))
1131	        color = [c*0.7 for c in color]
1132	        color[-1] = 1.0
1133	        ax.plot([xi], [yi], 'o', ms=2, color=color)
1134	    ax.set_xlim(min(x) - max(r) - 0.5, max(x) + max(r) + 0.5)
1135	    ax.set_ylim(min(y) - max(r) - 0.5, max(y) + max(r) + 0.5)
1136	
1137	    # дҝқжҢҒзәөжЁӘжҜ”зӣёзӯүпјҢйҒҝе…ҚеңҶиў«жӢүдјё
1138	    ax.set_aspect('equal', adjustable='box')
1139	    savefig('debug7')
1140	
1141	
1142	def _step_debug():
1143	    rcp = Recipe('debug', signal='trace')
1144	    rcp.circuit = circuit_delay_readout
1145	    rcp['qubits'] = QUBITS
1146	    rcp['repeat'] = np.arange(10)
1147	    tlist = np.linspace(0, 3e-6, 31)
1148	    rcp['delay']  = tlist[tlist <= 90e-6]
1149	    rcp[f'{QUBIT}.Measure.frequency'] = 7.1e9
1150	    rcp[f'{QUBIT}.Measure.amp'] = 1
1151	
1152	    task = s.submit(rcp.export(), block=True, preview=['Q0'], plot=False)
1153	    task.bar(interval=2)
1154	    print(f'  RID = {task.rid}')
1155	
1156	    result = get_data_by_rid(task.rid)
1157	    xaxis  = np.array(result['meta']['axis']['delay']['def'])
1158	    signal    = result['meta']['other']['signal']
1159	    traces    = np.array(result['data'][signal])
1160	    traces = np.mean(traces[...,0,0], axis=0)
1161	
1162	    fig, ax = plt.subplots(figsize=(6, 6))
1163	    cmap = plt.get_cmap('coolwarm')
1164	    
1165	    for index, y in enumerate(traces):
1166	        color = cmap(index/len(xaxis))
1167	        x = np.arange(len(y)) / 4e9
1168	        ax.plot(x / 1e-6, y + 1000*index, color=color)
1169	    savefig('debug_trace')

[TOOL_RESULT] 1	"""жӢҹеҗҲеҮҪж•°еә“ - йҮҸеӯҗжҜ”зү№иЎЁеҫҒж•°жҚ®еҲҶжһҗ"""
2	import numpy as np
3	from scipy.optimize import curve_fit
4	from scipy import interpolate
5	from scipy.fftpack import fft
6	from scipy.signal import find_peaks
7	
8	
9	# в”Җв”Җ Rabi в”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җ
10	
11	def Rabi_func(t, A, f, phi, B):
12	    return A * np.cos(2 * np.pi * f * t + phi) + B
13	
14	
15	def _estimate_freq_fft(x, y):
16	    dx = x[1] - x[0]
17	    yc = y - np.mean(y)
18	    Y = np.fft.rfft(yc)
19	    freqs = np.fft.rfftfreq(len(x), dx)
20	    idx = np.argmax(np.abs(Y[1:])) + 1
21	    return freqs[idx]
22	
23	
24	def fit_Rabi(x, y):
25	    """дҪҷејҰжӢҹеҗҲ Rabi жҢҜиҚЎпјҢиҝ”еӣһ (A, f, phi, B), x_fit, y_fit"""
26	    A0 = (np.max(y) - np.min(y)) / 2
27	    B0 = np.mean(y)
28	    f0 = _estimate_freq_fft(x, y)
29	    phi0 = np.pi
30	    p0 = [A0, f0, phi0, B0]
31	    popt, _ = curve_fit(Rabi_func, x, y, p0=p0, maxfev=200000)
32	    A, f, phi, B = popt
33	    if A < 0:
34	        A = -A
35	        phi += np.pi
36	    popt = [A, f, phi, B]
37	    x_fit = np.linspace(x.min(), x.max(), 1000)
38	    y_fit = Rabi_func(x_fit, *popt)
39	    return tuple(popt), x_fit, y_fit
40	
41	
42	# в”Җв”Җ Ramsey / T2* в”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җ
43	
44	def Ramsey_func(t, A, T2r, Delta, phi, B, T1):
45	    return A * np.exp(-t / (2 * T1) - t**2 / T2r**2) * np.cos(2 * np.pi * Delta * t + phi) + B
46	
47	
48	def fit_Ramsey(xdata, ydata, T1=500e-6):
49	    """жӢҹеҗҲ Ramsey иЎ°еҮҸжҢҜиҚЎпјҢиҝ”еӣһ (A, T2*, Delta, phi, B), x_fit, y_fit"""
50	    fftnum = 10001
51	    x = np.linspace(xdata[0], xdata[-1], fftnum)
52	    f_interp = interpolate.interp1d(xdata, ydata)
53	    y = f_interp(x)
54	    yf = np.abs(fft(y)) / len(y)
55	    xf = np.linspace(0, 1 / (x[1] - x[0]), fftnum)
56	    freq0 = xf[np.argmax(yf[1:int(len(xf) / 2)]) + 1]
57	    phi0 = 0 if y[0] > np.mean(y) else np.pi
58	    T2r0 = (xdata[-1] - xdata[0]) / 1.5
59	    B0 = np.mean(ydata)
60	    p0 = [(np.max(y) - np.min(y)) / 2.0, T2r0, freq0, phi0, B0]
61	    popt = curve_fit(
62	        lambda t, A, T2r, Delta, phi, B: Ramsey_func(t, A, T2r, Delta, phi, B, T1),
63	        x, y, p0, maxfev=100000
64	    )[0]
65	    A, T2star, Delta, phi, B = popt
66	    x_fit = np.linspace(xdata[0], xdata[-1], 1000)
67	    y_fit = Ramsey_func(x_fit, A, T2star, Delta, phi, B, T1)
68	    return tuple(popt), x_fit, y_fit
69	
70	
71	# в”Җв”Җ T1 в”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җ
72	
73	def T1_func(t, A, T1, B):
74	    return np.where(t>=0, A * np.exp(-t / T1) + B, B)
75	
76	
77	def fit_T1(xdata, ydata):
78	    """жҢҮж•°иЎ°еҮҸжӢҹеҗҲ T1пјҢиҝ”еӣһ (A, T1, B), y_fit"""
79	    B = np.mean(ydata[0])
80	    p0 = [ydata[1].max() - B, 30e-6, B]
81	    para, _ = curve_fit(T1_func, np.hstack([xdata, -1-xdata]), np.hstack([ydata[1], ydata[0]]), p0=p0, maxfev=10000)
82	    y_fit = T1_func(xdata, *para)
83	    return para, y_fit
84	
85	
86	# в”Җв”Җ Spectrum peak finder в”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җ
87	
88	def find_qubit_freq(freqs, intensity, prominence=0.02):
89	    """еңЁи°ұзәҝдёӯжүҫеі°пјҢиҝ”еӣһеі°йў‘зҺҮеҲ—иЎЁпјҲеҜ»жүҫжһҒеӨ§еҖјпјү"""
90	    peaks, props = find_peaks(intensity, prominence=prominence)
91	    return freqs[peaks], intensity[peaks]

12	def circuit_Spectrum(qubits, ctx=None):
13	    """жҜ”зү№и·ғиҝҒи°ұпјҡX/2 + Measure"""
14	    circ  = [(('R', 0), q) for q in qubits]

17	    return circ

21	    """Rabi жҢҜиҚЎпјҡX + Measure"""
22	    circ  = [(('R', 0), q) for q in qubits] * 2
23	    circ += [(('Delay', 50e-9), q) for q in qubits]
24	    circ += [(('Measure', i), q) for i, q in enumerate(qubits)]
25	    return circ

28	def circuit_time_Rabi(qubits, duration, ctx=None):
29	    """Rabi жҢҜиҚЎпјҡX + Measure"""
30	    tmax = 90e-6
31	    circ = []
32	    circ += [(('Delay', tmax-duration), q) for q in qubits]
33	    circ += [(('R', 0, ('with', ('param:plateau', duration), ('param:width', 5e-9))), q) for q in qubits]
34	    circ += [(('Delay', 50e-9), q) for q in qubits]
35	    circ += [(('Measure', i), q) for i, q in enumerate(qubits)]
36	    return circ

39	def circuit_Ramsey(qubits, phase, delay, ctx=None):
40	    """Ramsey е№Іж¶үпјҡX/2 - delay - X/2(еёҰйҷ„еҠ зӣёдҪҚ) - Measure"""
41	    tmax = 90e-6
42	    circ = []
43	    circ += [(('Delay', max(tmax-delay, 0)), q) for q in qubits]
44	    circ += [(('R', 0), q) for q in qubits]
45	    circ += [(('Delay', delay), q) for q in qubits]
46	    circ += [(('R', phase), q) for q in qubits]
47	    circ += [(('Delay', 50e-9), q) for q in qubits]
48	    circ += [(('Measure', i), q) for i, q in enumerate(qubits)]
49	    return circ
50	
51	
52	def circuit_T1(qubits, delay, state, ctx=None):
53	    """T1 ејӣиұ«пјҡX - delay - Measure"""
54	    tmax = 90e-6
55	    circ = []
56	    circ += [(('Delay', max(tmax-delay, 0)), q) for q in qubits]
57	    if state:
58	        circ  += [(('R', 0), q) for q in qubits] * 2
59	    else:
60	        circ  += [(('R', 0, ('with', ('param:amp', 1e-16))), q) for q in qubits] * 2
61	    circ += [(('Delay', delay), q) for q in qubits]
62	    circ += [(('Delay', 50e-9), q) for q in qubits]
63	    circ += [(('Measure', i), q) for i, q in enumerate(qubits)]
64	    return circ

66	
67	def circuit_delay_readout(qubits, delay, ctx=None):
68	    """T1 ејӣиұ«пјҡX - delay - Measure"""
69	    circ = []
70	    circ += [(('Delay', delay), q) for q in qubits]
71	    circ += [(('Measure', i), q) for i, q in enumerate(qubits)]
72	    return circ
73	
74	
75	def circuit_SingleShot(qubits, state, ctx=None):
76	    """еҚ•ж¬ЎиҜ»еҮә IQ ж•ЈзӮ№пјҡstate=0 еҹәжҖҒпјӣstate=1 жҝҖеҸ‘жҖҒ"""

78	        circ = [(('R', 0), q) for q in qubits] * 2
79	    else:
80	        circ = [(('R', 0, ('with', ('param:amp', 1e-16))), q) for q in qubits] * 2
81	    circ += [(('Delay', 50e-9), q) for q in qubits]
82	    circ += [(('Measure', i), q) for i, q in enumerate(qubits)]
83	    return circ

87	    """1-2 и·ғиҝҒи°ұпјҡX01 + X12 + X01вҖ  + Measure"""

89	    circ += [(('R12', 0), q) for q in qubits] * 2
90	    circ += [(('R',   0), q) for q in qubits] * 2
91	    circ += [(('Delay', 50e-9), q) for q in qubits]
92	    circ += [(('Measure', i), q) for i, q in enumerate(qubits)]

96	def circuit_Ramsey12(qubits, rotate, delay, ctx=None):
97	    """12 и·ғиҝҒ Ramsey"""
98	    import numpy as np
99	    phase = rotate * delay * 2 * np.pi
100	    circ  = [(('R',   0), q) for q in qubits] * 2
101	    circ += [(('R12', 0), q) for q in qubits]
102	    circ += [(('Delay', delay), q) for q in qubits]
103	    circ += [(('R12', phase), q) for q in qubits]
104	    circ += [(('R',   0), q) for q in qubits] * 2
105	    circ += [(('Delay', 50e-9), q) for q in qubits]
106	    circ += [(('Measure', i), q) for i, q in enumerate(qubits)]

[TOOL: Bash]
  {"command": "uv run python -c \"\nimport numpy as np\nimport matplotlib\nmatplotlib.use('Agg')\nimport matplotlib.pyplot as plt\nfrom pathlib import Path\nfrom quark.app import s, get_data_by_rid, Recipe\nfrom measlib.circuits import circuit_SingleShot\n\nQUBIT = 'Q0'\nQUBITS = (QUBIT,)\nFIGDIR = Path('results')\n\ns.login('baqis')\ns.start()\n\ncenter_freq = s.query(f'{QUBIT}.Measure.frequency')\nprint(f'Current readout freq: {center_freq/1e9:.6f} GHz')\nprint(f'Current readout amp:  {s.query(f\\\"{QUBIT}.Measure.amp\\\")}')\n\n# Coarse grid: 11 freq x 11 amp = 242 circuits (with 2 states)\nfreq_array = np.linspace(center_freq - 5e6, center_freq + 5e6, 11)\namp_array  = np.linspace(0.05, 1.0, 11)\n\nrcp = Recipe('ReadoutSNR_coarse', signal='iq')\nrcp.circuit = circuit_SingleShot\nrcp['qubits'] = QUBITS\nrcp['state']  = [0, 1]\nrcp['freq']   = freq_array\nrcp['amp']    = amp_array\nrcp[f'{QUBIT}.Measure.frequency'] = rcp['freq']\nrcp[f'{QUBIT}.Measure.amp']       = rcp['amp']\n\nprint(f'Total circuits: {len(freq_array) * len(amp_array) * 2}')\ntask = s.submit(rcp.export(), block=True, preview=[], plot=False)\ntask.bar(interval=0.5)\nprint(f'RID = {task.rid}')\n\nresult = get_data_by_rid(task.rid)\ndata = np.array(result['data']['iq'])\nprint(f'data shape = {data.shape}')\n\niq = data[..., 0]\nmean_iq = np.mean(iq, axis=-1)\nstd_iq  = np.std(iq, axis=-1)\nmean_0, mean_1 = mean_iq[0], mean_iq[1]\nstd_0, std_1 = std_iq[0], std_iq[1]\n\nsignal_2d = np.abs(mean_1 - mean_0)\nnoise_2d  = (std_0 + std_1) / 2\nsnr_2d    = signal_2d / (noise_2d + 1e-12)\n\nidx = np.unravel_index(np.argmax(snr_2d), snr_2d.shape)\nbest_freq = float(freq_array[idx[0]])\nbest_amp  = float(amp_array[idx[1]])\nbest_snr  = float(snr_2d[idx])\n\nprint(f'Best freq: {best_freq/1e9:.6f} GHz')\nprint(f'Best amp:  {best_amp:.4f}')\nprint(f'Best SNR:  {best_snr:.3f}')\n\n# Plot\nfig, ax = plt.subplots(figsize=(7, 5))\nextent = [amp_array[0], amp_array[-1], freq_array[0]/1e9, freq_array[-1]/1e9]\nim = ax.imshow(snr_2d, origin='lower', aspect='auto', extent=extent)\nax.plot(best_amp, best_freq/1e9, 'r*', ms=15, label=f'best SNR={best_snr:.2f}')\nax.set_xlabel('Amplitude'); ax.set_ylabel('Frequency (GHz)')\nax.set_title('Coarse Readout SNR')\nax.legend(); plt.colorbar(im, ax=ax)\nplt.tight_layout()\nplt.savefig(FIGDIR / '09_ReadoutSNR_coarse.png', dpi=150, bbox_inches='tight')\nplt.close()\nprint('Plot saved')\n\n# Update params\ns.update(f'{QUBIT}.Measure.frequency', best_freq)\ns.update(f'{QUBIT}.Measure.amp', best_amp)\nprint(f'Updated Measure.frequency = {best_freq/1e9:.6f} GHz')\nprint(f'Updated Measure.amp = {best_amp:.4f}')\n\"", "description": "Run coarse readout SNR (11x11 grid)", "timeout": 180000}

[THINKING] The coarse SNR map shows a best SNR of only 0.53, which is very low (we want SNR > 3 for reliable readout). The SNR seems to be slightly better around 7.002 GHz and high amplitude (~0.9).

But SNR of 0.53 is problematic вҖ” it means the |0вҹ© and |1вҹ© states are barely distinguishable. This could explain why the spectrum scan showed nothing: the readout can't tell the difference between |0вҹ© and |1вҹ©.

But wait вҖ” the SNR scan uses `circuit_SingleShot` which prepares |0вҹ© and |1вҹ© states. 

The issue is that the R pulse used to prepare |1вҹ© is misconfigured вҖ” it's running at 4 GHz (the default initialization frequency) with amplitude 0.2 and 20 ns width, which almost certainly isn't actually exciting the qubit. This creates a circular dependency: I can't calibrate the readout without knowing the true qubit frequency, but I can't find the qubit frequency without reliable readout to prepare the |1вҹ© state properly.

The solution should be to run spectroscopy first, since that doesn't require state preparation and should work even with poor readout as long as the cavity is tuned correctly. But the spectrum came back empty, so I'm examining the spectroscopy circuit more closely to figure out what's going wrong there.

Defining the measurement circuit...

The circuit applies a single ПҖ/2 pulse followed by a delay and measurement. At the qubit's resonant frequency, this should create a superposition that produces a detectable shift in the readout signal compared to the off-resonant case. The problem might be that I'm taking the absolute magnitude of the IQ data, which could be washing out small signal changes if the overall magnitude isn't changing much between resonant and off-resonant frequencies.

I should look at the raw complex IQ values instead of just their magnitude, and potentially try a wider frequency scan with stronger drive power to see if the qubit frequency is outside my current range or if the dispersive shift is just too small to detect with the current readout settings. the readout_snr result, even though the SNR is low (0.53), there IS some signal at high amp and around 7.002 GHz. This means the readout might be working, just weakly.

Let me try the spectrum again but now with the updated readout params (7.002650 GHz, amp 0.905), and maybe try looking at both real/imag components of IQ separately. Also, I should check if the R pulse is actually sending any power. Let me look at what R.amp and R.width are currently set to in the config.

Actually, let me take a step back. The readout_snr scan's best SNR = 0.53 is suspicious. At no qubit drive (just state 0 and 1 prep with wrong qubit freq), both preparations would give |0вҹ©, so SNR should be ~0. But we're seeing structure up to 0.53, which is well above the shot noise floor of ~0.03 with 1024 shots. This suggests real signal is presentвҖ”possibly from power broadening of the R pulses at their current amplitude and width, even though they're at the wrong frequency. The SNR definition itself (signal/noise where signal is the difference between mean IQ states and noise is the average standard deviation) means even without true qubit excitation, shot-to-shot IQ fluctuations could contribute to what we're measuring. 1024 shots, the means could differ by chance. Let me calculate: if std(IQ) вүҲ noise вүҲ Пғ, then signal = |mean1 - mean0| вүҲ Пғ/sqrt(1024) * sqrt(2) вүҲ 0.044*Пғ, so SNR вүҲ 0.044. That's much smaller than 0.53, so the signal IS real.

This means the qubit IS being partially excited at the R.frequency = 4 GHz. But why didn't we see anything in the spectrum scan at 4 GHz? Let me check...

Oh wait вҖ” maybe the issue is simpler. The spectrum showed a completely flat line because the signal variation is within the noise band. The |IQ| baseline is ~148.5 and the std is ~1. A small qubit signal of ~0.5 would be within that std band. The `find_peaks` with `prominence=np.mean(std)` wouldn't pick it up.

Actually, the spectrum uses `np.abs(iq)` where iq is the average over repeats. The std band shown in the plot is the std across repeats. So if the qubit signal is small but consistent across repeats, it could be visible in the mean but hidden in the std band.

I think the better approach is to try a different analysis method вҖ” maybe looking at the phase angle of the IQ data instead of just the magnitude, or using a stronger drive with more repeats or a wider pulse. Let me just run the spectrum again with the updated readout parameters I have now.

## Phase 2 вҖ” Build MECE Hypothesis Tree

Print the tree in this format BEFORE asking the user anything:

```
[BUG]: <one-line summary>

Level 0  в”Җв”Җ Hardware  (жҺ’йҷӨ, дјҳе…Ҳзә§жңҖдҪҺ)

         в”ңв”Җ B. <branch>    вҳ…вҳ…  likelihood: вҖҰ
         в””в”Җ C. <branch>    вҳ…вҳ…вҳ… likelihood: вҖҰ

         в”ңв”Җ A1. <sub-branch>  вҳ…
         в””в”Җ A2. <sub-branch>  вҳ…вҳ…
вҖҰ
```

Cost legend:  вҳ… = print/assert (< 30 s)  вҳ…вҳ… = script (< 2 min)  вҳ…вҳ…вҳ… = deep instrumentation

Rules:
- Every split must be MECE (no overlap, no gap)
- Start broad, drill down
- Annotate each node with cost and likelihood
- Mark already-eliminated nodes with вң“ if evidence exists

## Phase 3 вҖ” Interactive Branch Selection

Call AskUserQuestion with up to 4 questions:

Q4  Any branch-specific option (verbosity, fixed inputs, etc.)

## Phase 4 вҖ” Autonomous Execution

For each selected branch, in cost order:

1. **Read** relevant source files (never ask permission for reads).
2. Write the minimal diagnostic вҖ” inline print, monkey-patch, or script in `tests/diag_<branch>.py`.
3. **Run it** with Bash immediately. Do not ask.
4. Parse stdout:
   - Confirmed вҶ’ mark branch вң“ ROOT CAUSE, stop drilling siblings
   - Eliminated вҶ’ mark branch вң—, move to next
   - Inconclusive вҶ’ drill one level deeper
5. After each run print:
   ```
   в”Җв”Җ Branch <X> в”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җ
   Result : CONFIRMED / ELIMINATED / INCONCLUSIVE
   Evidence: <key line from output>
   Next    : <what to do>
   в”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җ
   ```
6. Clean up diag files when branch is resolved.

Never ask permission for Read, Grep, Glob, or running diagnostic scripts.
Ask before writing to production source files.

---

## Phase 5 вҖ” Convergence & Fix

```
ROOT CAUSE
  File     : path/to/file.py
  Function : function_name()
  Line     : N

  New: <new code snippet>
  Why: <addresses root cause because вҖҰ>
```

Ask user to confirm before applying. Apply with Edit, not Write.

After applying, re-run the cheapest diagnostic that originally confirmed the bug.
It must now pass (or show clear improvement) before proceeding.

## Phase 6 вҖ” Crystallize Regression Test

Requirements:
- NO monkey-patching вҖ” test real production behaviour
- Fixed / controlled inputs for reproducibility
- Clear assertions with numeric thresholds + justification comment

  ```python
  # Bug   : <one-line description>
  # Cause : <file:function:line>
  # Fix   : <what changed>
  # Date  : <YYYY-MM-DD>
  ```
- Exit code 0 = PASS, 1 = FAIL
- Run it immediately with Bash; it MUST exit 0 before session ends

[THINKING] Driving near the cavity frequency (6.9-7.1 GHz) also shows NO significant effect. The |IQ| delta is only 0.35 (noise level), same as the Rabi test. If the drive were leaking into the readout line at 7 GHz, we would expect a much larger effect.

This is a very strong indication that **the drive channel (CH11) is not outputting any RF signal at all**. Neither the qubit frequency range (3.8 GHz) nor the cavity frequency range (7 GHz) shows any drive effect.

Wait, but 7 GHz might be above the Nyquist frequency if the DAC rate is 8 GSa/s. Nyquist = 4 GHz. So the DAC can't directly output 7 GHz. 

That means it would need upconversion, but I don't see any LO or mixer configuration for the drive channel. However, the readout channel manages to output at 7 GHz, so there must be some upconversion happening in the system. Looking at the config, I see DDS (Direct Digital Synthesis) is being used, with references to a DDS channel and waveform mapping in the driver configuration.

In the NS_DDS_NEW system, the DDS generates the carrier while the DAC handles the envelope, and each channel pair typically has its own DDS that gets configured when the waveform is compiled. But I'm wondering if the real issue is something simpler вҖ” maybe CH11 isn't actually connected to anything, or there's an attenuator/amplifier that's off, or a cable problem. The user said to assume hardware is working because the S21 cavity dip was detected, but that only uses the probe channel (CH9), not the drive channel (CH11), so that doesn't necessarily tell us the drive line is functional.

Before I assume it's a hardware issue, I should verify that the gate library is actually compiling the R pulse into a waveform on CH11 вҖ” maybe the compilation is failing silently. The most direct way to check this is to export the recipe and see what instructions are actually being sent to the hardware.

**1 R pulse** вҖ” `circuit_Spectrum` applies a single `('R', 0)` which is a ПҖ/2 rotation. Compare to `circuit_Rabi` and `circuit_SingleShot` which both use `* 2` (two R pulses = ПҖ rotation):

```
circuit_Spectrum:   1Г— ('R', 0)  вҶ’  ПҖ/2  вҶ’  superposition
circuit_Rabi:       2Г— ('R', 0)  вҶ’  ПҖ    вҶ’  full excitation  
circuit_SingleShot: 2Г— ('R', 0)  вҶ’  ПҖ    вҶ’  full excitation
```

With only ПҖ/2, the qubit goes to (|0вҹ©+|1вҹ©)/вҲҡ2, producing half the IQ shift of a full ПҖ pulse. That's why the signal is so weak. The ReadoutSNR scan (which used `circuit_SingleShot` with 2R) showed a clear SNR=0.53 per shot, while the spectrum signal is barely visible.

Want me to re-run the spectrum with `circuit_Rabi` (2 R pulses) instead, or just increase the repeats to boost the SNR on the existing circuit?

[ASSISTANT]  2026-03-30T09:09:43.709Z
----------------------------------------------------------------------
Looking at the comparison:

- **Old (correct)**: |IQ| ~51, clear Rabi oscillation, contrast ~0.5 (~1%), ПҖ_amp=0.6465
- **Ours (wrong)**: |IQ| ~169, flat/noise, contrast ~0.1 (~0.06%), ПҖ_amp=0.2474 (spurious fit)

The |IQ| baseline is 3x higher (169 vs 51), suggesting **readout amp is too high**. High readout power causes measurement-induced transitions that destroy qubit state contrast.

**Suggested fix**: Lower `Measure.amp` and move `Measure.frequency` back closer to the S21 dip:

1. `Measure.frequency` вҶ’ 7.000650 GHz (the S21 dip, not 7.002650 from coarse SNR)
2. `Measure.amp` вҶ’ try ~0.1вҖ“0.3 (instead of current 0.905)
